  `description` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `classement` enum('Privé','Partagé') COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT 'Privé',

  `piece_jointes` json DEFAULT NULL,
  `date_debut_agenda` date DEFAULT NULL,
  `heure_debut_agenda` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,

  `heure_fin_agenda` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `bg_color` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `created_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `deleted_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `agendas_user_id_foreign` (`user_id`),
  CONSTRAINT `agendas_user_id_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`user_id`) REFERENCES `users` (`id`) ON DELETE SET NULL
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=2 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;

-- Listage de la structure de table dna_mps. certifications
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `certifications` (
  `id` bigint unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `user_id` bigint unsigned NOT NULL,
  `module_pedagogique_id` bigint unsigned DEFAULT NULL,
  `parcours_id` bigint unsigned DEFAULT NULL,
  `numero_unique` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `verification_token` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `date_emission` date NOT NULL,
  `date_expiration` date DEFAULT NULL,
  `statut` enum('actif','expire','revoque') COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT 'actif',
  `pdf_path` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `certification_parent_id` bigint unsigned DEFAULT NULL,
  `deleted_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `created_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  UNIQUE KEY `certifications_numero_unique_unique` (`numero_unique`),
  UNIQUE KEY `certifications_verification_token_unique` (`verification_token`),
  KEY `certifications_user_id_foreign` (`user_id`),
  KEY `certifications_module_pedagogique_id_foreign` (`module_pedagogique_id`),
  KEY `certifications_parcours_id_foreign` (`parcours_id`),
  KEY `certifications_certification_parent_id_foreign` (`certification_parent_id`),
  CONSTRAINT `certifications_certification_parent_id_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`certification_parent_id`) REFERENCES `certifications` (`id`) ON DELETE SET NULL,
  CONSTRAINT `certifications_module_pedagogique_id_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`module_pedagogique_id`) REFERENCES `module_pedagogiques` (`id`) ON DELETE SET NULL,
  CONSTRAINT `certifications_parcours_id_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`parcours_id`) REFERENCES `parcours` (`id`) ON DELETE SET NULL,
  CONSTRAINT `certifications_user_id_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`user_id`) REFERENCES `users` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;

-- Listage de la structure de table dna_mps. conversation_user
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `conversation_user` (
  `id` bigint unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `conversation_id` bigint unsigned NOT NULL,
  `user_id` bigint unsigned NOT NULL,
  `last_read_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `created_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  UNIQUE KEY `conversation_user_conversation_id_user_id_unique` (`conversation_id`,`user_id`),
  KEY `conversation_user_user_id_foreign` (`user_id`),
  CONSTRAINT `conversation_user_conversation_id_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`conversation_id`) REFERENCES `conversations` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  CONSTRAINT `conversation_user_user_id_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`user_id`) REFERENCES `users` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=60 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;

-- Listage de la structure de table dna_mps. documents
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `documents` (
  `id` bigint unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `cree_par_id` bigint unsigned NOT NULL,
  `parent_id` bigint unsigned DEFAULT NULL,
  `nom` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `type` enum('fichier','dossier') COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT 'fichier',
  `description` text COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci,
  `chemin_stockage` varchar(1024) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `nom_original` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `mime_type` varchar(100) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `taille` bigint unsigned DEFAULT NULL,
  `est_public` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `public_token` varchar(64) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `public_permissions` json DEFAULT NULL,
  `is_archive` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `deleted_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `created_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  UNIQUE KEY `uq_nom_parent` (`parent_id`,`nom`),
  UNIQUE KEY `documents_public_token_unique` (`public_token`),
  KEY `documents_cree_par_id_index` (`cree_par_id`),
  KEY `documents_parent_id_index` (`parent_id`),
  KEY `documents_type_index` (`type`),
  KEY `documents_est_public_index` (`est_public`),
  KEY `documents_created_at_index` (`created_at`),
  CONSTRAINT `documents_cree_par_id_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`cree_par_id`) REFERENCES `users` (`id`) ON DELETE RESTRICT,
  CONSTRAINT `documents_parent_id_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`parent_id`) REFERENCES `documents` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=332 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;

-- Listage de la structure de table dna_mps. document_shares
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `document_shares` (
  `id` bigint unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `document_id` bigint unsigned NOT NULL,
  `user_id` bigint unsigned DEFAULT NULL,
  `groupe_id` bigint unsigned DEFAULT NULL,
  `email` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `token` varchar(64) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `permissions` json DEFAULT NULL,
  `message` text COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci,
  `shared_by_id` bigint unsigned NOT NULL,
  `expires_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `accepted_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `created_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `deleted_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  UNIQUE KEY `document_shares_token_unique` (`token`),
  KEY `document_shares_document_id_foreign` (`document_id`),
  KEY `document_shares_user_id_foreign` (`user_id`),
  KEY `document_shares_shared_by_id_foreign` (`shared_by_id`),
  KEY `document_shares_email_token_index` (`email`,`token`),
  KEY `document_shares_groupe_id_foreign` (`groupe_id`),
  CONSTRAINT `document_shares_document_id_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`document_id`) REFERENCES `documents` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  CONSTRAINT `document_shares_groupe_id_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`groupe_id`) REFERENCES `groupes` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  CONSTRAINT `document_shares_shared_by_id_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`shared_by_id`) REFERENCES `users` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  CONSTRAINT `document_shares_user_id_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`user_id`) REFERENCES `users` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=66 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;

-- Listage de la structure de table dna_mps. faqs
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `faqs` (
  `id` bigint unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `question` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `reponse` text COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `slug` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `categorie` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `statut` enum('brouillon','publie','archive') COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT 'brouillon',
  `publie_le` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `votes_utiles` int unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `votes_inutiles` int unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `created_by` bigint unsigned DEFAULT NULL,
  `created_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `deleted_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  UNIQUE KEY `faqs_slug_unique` (`slug`),
  KEY `faqs_created_by_foreign` (`created_by`),
  KEY `faqs_categorie_index` (`categorie`),
  KEY `faqs_statut_index` (`statut`),
  CONSTRAINT `faqs_created_by_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`created_by`) REFERENCES `users` (`id`) ON DELETE SET NULL
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;

  `id` bigint unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `user_id` bigint unsigned DEFAULT NULL,
  `action` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,

  `nouvelle_valeur` json DEFAULT NULL,
  `ip` varchar(45) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,

  `route` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,

  `created_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `journal_audits_user_id_foreign` (`user_id`),
  KEY `journal_audits_auditable_type_auditable_id_index` (`auditable_type`,`auditable_id`),
  KEY `journal_audits_action_index` (`action`),

) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=60 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;

-- Listage de la structure de table dna_mps. lecons
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `lecons` (
  `id` bigint unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `module_pedagogique_id` bigint unsigned NOT NULL,
  `titre` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `type` enum('standard','interactif','evaluation') COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT 'standard',
  `obligatoire` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '1',
  `ordre` int NOT NULL,
  `created_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `deleted_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `description` longtext COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci,
  `questions_interactives` json DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `lecons_module_pedagogique_id_foreign` (`module_pedagogique_id`),
  CONSTRAINT `lecons_module_pedagogique_id_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`module_pedagogique_id`) REFERENCES `module_pedagogiques` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=2 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;

-- Listage des données de la table dna_mps.lecons : ~0 rows (environ)

-- Listage de la structure de table dna_mps. messages
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `messages` (
  `id` bigint unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `conversation_id` bigint unsigned NOT NULL,
  `user_id` bigint unsigned NOT NULL,
  `content` text COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `file_path` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `file_name` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `file_size` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `file_mime` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `type` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT 'text',
  `created_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `document_id` bigint unsigned DEFAULT NULL,
  `parent_id` bigint unsigned DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `messages_conversation_id_foreign` (`conversation_id`),
  KEY `messages_user_id_foreign` (`user_id`),
  KEY `messages_document_id_foreign` (`document_id`),
  KEY `messages_parent_id_foreign` (`parent_id`),
  CONSTRAINT `messages_conversation_id_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`conversation_id`) REFERENCES `conversations` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  CONSTRAINT `messages_document_id_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`document_id`) REFERENCES `documents` (`id`) ON DELETE SET NULL,
  CONSTRAINT `messages_parent_id_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`parent_id`) REFERENCES `messages` (`id`) ON DELETE SET NULL,
  CONSTRAINT `messages_user_id_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`user_id`) REFERENCES `users` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=152 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;

-- Listage de la structure de table dna_mps. progressions
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `progressions` (
  `id` bigint unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `user_id` bigint unsigned NOT NULL,
  `parcour_id` bigint unsigned DEFAULT NULL,
  `module_pedagogique_id` bigint unsigned DEFAULT NULL,
  `lecon_id` bigint unsigned DEFAULT NULL,
  `quiz_id` bigint unsigned DEFAULT NULL,
  `temps_passe` int NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `last_timecode_video` int unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `est_terminee` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `taux_progression` decimal(5,2) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0.00',
  `date_completion` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `deleted_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `created_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `progressions_module_pedagogique_id_foreign` (`module_pedagogique_id`),
  KEY `progressions_lecon_id_foreign` (`lecon_id`),
  KEY `progressions_quiz_id_foreign` (`quiz_id`),
  KEY `progressions_user_id_foreign` (`user_id`),
  KEY `progressions_parcour_id_foreign` (`parcour_id`),
  CONSTRAINT `progressions_lecon_id_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`lecon_id`) REFERENCES `lecons` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  CONSTRAINT `progressions_module_pedagogique_id_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`module_pedagogique_id`) REFERENCES `module_pedagogiques` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  CONSTRAINT `progressions_parcour_id_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`parcour_id`) REFERENCES `parcours` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  CONSTRAINT `progressions_quiz_id_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`quiz_id`) REFERENCES `quizzes` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  CONSTRAINT `progressions_user_id_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`user_id`) REFERENCES `users` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;

-- Listage de la structure de table dna_mps. ptms
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `ptms` (
  `id` bigint unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `ptt_id` bigint unsigned NOT NULL,
  `titre_ptm` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `description_ptm` text COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci,
  `date_debut_ptm` date DEFAULT NULL,
  `date_fin_ptm` date DEFAULT NULL,
  `responsable_ptm_id` int DEFAULT NULL,
  `statut_ptm` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `created_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `deleted_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `ptms_ptt_id_foreign` (`ptt_id`),
  CONSTRAINT `ptms_ptt_id_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`ptt_id`) REFERENCES `ptts` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=14 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;

-- Listage de la structure de table dna_mps. ptts
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `ptts` (
  `id` bigint unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `ptba_id` bigint unsigned NOT NULL,
  `budget_alloue` double DEFAULT NULL,
  `responsable_ids` json DEFAULT NULL,
  `code_ptt` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `nom_ptt` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `numero_trimestre` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `date_debut` date DEFAULT NULL,
  `date_fin` date DEFAULT NULL,
  `statut` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `created_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `deleted_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `indicateur` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `objectif_ptt` text COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci,
  `resultat_attendu` text COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci,
  `activite_cle` text COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci,
  `trimestre` text COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `ptts_ptba_id_foreign` (`ptba_id`),
  CONSTRAINT `ptts_ptba_id_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`ptba_id`) REFERENCES `ptbas` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=92 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;

-- Listage de la structure de table dna_mps. questions
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `questions` (
  `id` bigint unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `thematique_id` bigint unsigned DEFAULT NULL,
  `quiz_id` bigint unsigned DEFAULT NULL,
  `enonce` text COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `type` enum('qcm','choix_unique','choix_multiple','vrai_faux','association','classement','glisser_deposer','reponse_courte','reponse_longue','question_ouverte','definition','explication','cas_pratique','probleme','exercice','analyse_document','calcul','code','orale','presentation','projet') COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `ordre` int NOT NULL,
  `deleted_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `created_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `explication` text COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `questions_quiz_id_foreign` (`quiz_id`),
  KEY `questions_thematique_id_foreign` (`thematique_id`),
  CONSTRAINT `questions_quiz_id_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`quiz_id`) REFERENCES `quizzes` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  CONSTRAINT `questions_thematique_id_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`thematique_id`) REFERENCES `thematiques` (`id`) ON DELETE SET NULL
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=2 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;

-- Listage de la structure de table dna_mps. quizzes
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `quizzes` (
  `id` bigint unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `module_pedagogique_id` bigint unsigned NOT NULL,
  `thematique_id` bigint unsigned DEFAULT NULL,
  `nb_questions_pool` int NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT 'Si > 0, tire X questions au hasard de la thématique',
  `titre` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `description` text COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci,
  `type` enum('standard','interactif','evaluation') COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT 'standard',
  `obligatoire` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '1',
  `seuil_reussite` tinyint unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '70',
  `tentative_max` tinyint unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '3',
  `ordre` int NOT NULL,
  `deleted_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `created_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `duree_limite` int DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `quizzes_module_pedagogique_id_foreign` (`module_pedagogique_id`),
  KEY `quizzes_thematique_id_foreign` (`thematique_id`),
  CONSTRAINT `quizzes_module_pedagogique_id_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`module_pedagogique_id`) REFERENCES `module_pedagogiques` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  CONSTRAINT `quizzes_thematique_id_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`thematique_id`) REFERENCES `thematiques` (`id`) ON DELETE SET NULL
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=2 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;

-- Listage de la structure de table dna_mps. reactions
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `reactions` (
  `id` bigint unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `message_id` bigint unsigned NOT NULL,
  `user_id` bigint unsigned NOT NULL,
  `emoji` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `created_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  UNIQUE KEY `reactions_message_id_user_id_emoji_unique` (`message_id`,`user_id`,`emoji`),
  KEY `reactions_user_id_foreign` (`user_id`),
  CONSTRAINT `reactions_message_id_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`message_id`) REFERENCES `messages` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  CONSTRAINT `reactions_user_id_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`user_id`) REFERENCES `users` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=45 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;

-- Listage de la structure de table dna_mps. reponse_attendues
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `reponse_attendues` (
  `id` bigint unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `question_id` bigint unsigned NOT NULL,
  `valeur` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `est_correcte` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `deleted_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `created_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `reponse_attendues_question_id_foreign` (`question_id`),
  CONSTRAINT `reponse_attendues_question_id_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`question_id`) REFERENCES `questions` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=4 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;

-- Listage de la structure de table dna_mps. reponse_soumises
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `reponse_soumises` (
  `id` bigint unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `tentative_quiz_id` bigint unsigned NOT NULL,
  `question_id` bigint unsigned NOT NULL,
  `valeur_saisie` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `correcte` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `deleted_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `created_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `reponse_soumises_tentative_quiz_id_foreign` (`tentative_quiz_id`),
  KEY `reponse_soumises_question_id_foreign` (`question_id`),
  CONSTRAINT `reponse_soumises_question_id_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`question_id`) REFERENCES `questions` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  CONSTRAINT `reponse_soumises_tentative_quiz_id_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`tentative_quiz_id`) REFERENCES `tentative_quizzes` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;

-- Listage de la structure de table dna_mps. ressources
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `ressources` (
  `id` bigint unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `lecon_id` bigint unsigned NOT NULL,
  `type` enum('video','image','audio','document','lien','texte','autre') COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `nom` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `url` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `contenu` longtext COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci,
  `taille` int DEFAULT NULL,
  `mime_type` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `hash` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `hash_fichier` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `ordre` int NOT NULL DEFAULT '1',
  `created_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `deleted_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `ressources_lecon_id_foreign` (`lecon_id`),
  CONSTRAINT `ressources_lecon_id_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`lecon_id`) REFERENCES `lecons` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=2 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;

-- Listage de la structure de table dna_mps. roles
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `roles` (
  `id` bigint unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `name` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `guard_name` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `created_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),

  `updated_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,

) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=7 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;
